    if (nrow(ipd) == 0) stop("There are no patients with valid weights in IPD!")

                    		
                  

                  

                    140
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    141
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    142
                    2x
                    
                      
  outcome_cols <- if (endpoint_type == "tte") c("TIME", "EVENT") else "RESPONSE"

                    		
                  

                  

                    143
                    2x
                    
                      
  retain_cols <- c("USUBJID", "ARM", outcome_cols, "weights")

                    		
                  

                  

                    144
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    145
                    2x
                    
                      
  ipd <- ipd[, retain_cols, drop = FALSE]

                    		
                  

                  

                    146
                    2x
                    
                      
  pseudo_ipd <- pseudo_ipd[, retain_cols, drop = FALSE]

                    		
                  

                  

                    147
                    2x
                    
                      
  dat <- rbind(ipd, pseudo_ipd) # only used if apply contrast method

                    		
                  

                  

                    148
                    2x
                    
                      
  ipd$ARM <- factor(ipd$ARM, levels = c(trt_common, trt_ipd))

                    		
                  

                  

                    149
                    2x
                    
                      
  pseudo_ipd$ARM <- factor(pseudo_ipd$ARM, levels = c(trt_common, trt_agd))

                    		
                  

                  

                    150
                    2x
                    
                      
  dat$ARM <- factor(dat$ARM, levels = c(trt_common, trt_agd, trt_ipd))

                    		
                  

                  

                    151
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    152
                    
                    
                      
  # ==> Inferential output ------------------------------------------

                    		
                  

                  

                    153
                    2x
                    
                      
  result <- if (endpoint_type == "tte") {

                    		
                  

                  

                    154
                    2x
                    
                      
    maic_anchored_tte(res, ipd, km_conf_type, pseudo_ipd, time_scale, weights_object, endpoint_name, trt_ipd, trt_agd)

                    		
                  

                  

                    155
                    
                    
                      
  } else {

                    		
                  

                  

                    156
                    !
                    
                      
    stop("Endpoint type ", endpoint_type, " currently unsupported.")

                    		
                  

                  

                    157
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    158
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    159
                    2x
                    
                      
  result

                    		
                  

                  

                    160
                    
                    
                      
}

                    		
                  

                  

                    161
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    162
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    163
                    
                    
                      
# MAIC inference functions by outcome type ------------

                    		
                  

                  

                    164
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    165
                    
                    
                      
maic_anchored_tte <- function(res,

                    		
                  

                  

                    166
                    
                    
                      
                              ipd,

                    		
                  

                  

                    167
                    
                    
                      
                              km_conf_type,

                    		
                  

                  

                    168
                    
                    
                      
                              pseudo_ipd,

                    		
                  

                  

                    169
                    
                    
                      
                              time_scale,

                    		
                  

                  

                    170
                    
                    
                      
                              weights_object,

                    		
                  

                  

                    171
                    
                    
                      
                              endpoint_name,

                    		
                  

                  

                    172
                    
                    
                      
                              trt_ipd,

                    		
                  

                  

                    173
                    
                    
                      
                              trt_agd) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    174
                    
                    
                      
  # Analysis table (Cox model) before and after matching, incl Median Survival Time

                    		
                  

                  

                    175
                    
                    
                      
  # derive km w and w/o weights

                    		
                  

                  

                    176
                    2x
                    
                      
  kmobj_ipd <- survfit(Surv(TIME, EVENT) ~ ARM, ipd, conf.type = km_conf_type)

                    		
                  

                  

                    177
                    2x
                    
                      
  kmobj_ipd_adj <- survfit(Surv(TIME, EVENT) ~ ARM, ipd, weights = ipd$weights, conf.type = km_conf_type)

                    		
                  

                  

                    178
                    2x
                    
                      
  kmobj_agd <- survfit(Surv(TIME, EVENT) ~ ARM, pseudo_ipd, conf.type = km_conf_type)

                    		
                  

                  

                    179
                    2x
                    
                      
  res$descriptive[["survfit_ipd_before"]] <- survfit_makeup(kmobj_ipd)

                    		
                  

                  

                    180
                    2x
                    
                      
  res$descriptive[["survfit_ipd_after"]] <- survfit_makeup(kmobj_ipd_adj)

                    		
                  

                  

                    181
                    2x
                    
                      
  res$descriptive[["survfit_pseudo"]] <- survfit_makeup(kmobj_agd)

                    		
                  

                  

                    182
                    
                    
                      
  # derive median survival time

                    		
                  

                  

                    183
                    2x
                    
                      
  medSurv_ipd <- medSurv_makeup(kmobj_ipd, legend = "IPD, before matching", time_scale = time_scale)

                    		
                  

                  

                    184
                    2x
                    
                      
  medSurv_ipd_adj <- medSurv_makeup(kmobj_ipd_adj, legend = "IPD, after matching", time_scale = time_scale)

                    		
                  

                  

                    185
                    2x
                    
                      
  medSurv_agd <- medSurv_makeup(kmobj_agd, legend = "AgD, external", time_scale = time_scale)

                    		
                  

                  

                    186
                    2x
                    
                      
  medSurv_out <- rbind(medSurv_ipd, medSurv_ipd_adj, medSurv_agd)

                    		
                  

                  

                    187
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    188
                    2x
                    
                      
  res$inferential[["report_median_surv"]] <- medSurv_out

                    		
                  

                  

                    189
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    190
                    
                    
                      
  # fit PH Cox regression model

                    		
                  

                  

                    191
                    2x
                    
                      
  coxobj_ipd <- coxph(Surv(TIME, EVENT) ~ ARM, ipd, robust = TRUE)

                    		
                  

                  

                    192
                    2x
                    
                      
  coxobj_ipd_adj <- coxph(Surv(TIME, EVENT) ~ ARM, ipd, weights = weights, robust = TRUE)

                    		
                  

                  

                    193
                    2x
                    
                      
  coxobj_agd <- coxph(Surv(TIME, EVENT) ~ ARM, pseudo_ipd, robust = TRUE)

                    		
                  

                  

                    194
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    195
                    2x
                    
                      
  res$inferential[["ipd_coxph_before"]] <- coxobj_ipd

                    		
                  

                  

                    196
                    2x
                    
                      
  res$inferential[["ipd_coxph_after"]] <- coxobj_ipd_adj

                    		
                  

                  

                    197
                    2x
                    
                      
  res$inferential[["agd_coxph"]] <- coxobj_agd

                    		
                  

                  

                    198
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    199
                    
                    
                      
  # derive ipd exp arm vs agd exp arm via bucher

                    		
                  

                  

                    200
                    2x
                    
                      
  res_AC <- as.list(summary(coxobj_ipd_adj)$coef)[c(1, 4)]

                    202
                    2x

                    2x
                    
                      
  res_AB <- bucher(res_AC, res_BC, conf_lv = 0.95)

                    		
                  

                  

                    204
                    2x
                    
                      
  res_AB$est <- exp(res_AB$est)

                    		
                  

                  

                    205
                    2x
                    
                      
  res_AB$ci_l <- exp(res_AB$ci_l)

                    		
                  

                  

                    206
                    2x
                    
                      
  res_AB$ci_u <- exp(res_AB$ci_u)

                    		
                  

                  

                    207
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    208
                    
                    
                      
  # get bootstrapped estimates if applicable

                    		
                  

                  

                    209
                    2x
                    
                      
  res$inferential[["boot_est"]] <- NULL

                    		
                  

                  

                    210
                    2x
                    
                      
  if (!is.null(weights_object$boot)) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    211
                    1x
                    
                      
    tmp_boot_obj <- weights_object$boot

                    		
                  

                  

                    212
                    1x
                    
                      
    k <- dim(tmp_boot_obj)[3]

                    		
                  

                  

                    213
                    1x
                    
                      
    tmp_boot_est <- sapply(seq_len(k), function(ii) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    214
                    5x
                    
                      
      boot_x <- tmp_boot_obj[, , ii]

                    		
                  

                  

                    215
                    5x
                    
                      
      boot_ipd_id <- weights_object$data$USUBJID[boot_x[, 1]]

                    		
                  

                  

                    216
                    5x
                    
                      
      boot_ipd <- ipd[match(boot_ipd_id, ipd$USUBJID), , drop = FALSE]

                    		
                  

                  

                    217
                    5x
                    
                      
      boot_ipd$weights <- boot_x[, 2]

                    		
                  

                  

                    218
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    219
                    
                    
                      
      # does not matter use robust se or not, point estimate will not change and calculation would be faster

                    		
                  

                  

                    220
                    5x
                    
                      
      boot_coxobj_ipd_adj <- coxph(Surv(TIME, EVENT) ~ ARM, boot_ipd, weights = weights)

                    		
                  

                  

                    221
                    5x
                    
                      
      boot_AB_est <- summary(boot_coxobj_ipd_adj)$coef[1] - summary(coxobj_agd)$coef[1]

                    		
                  

                  

                    222
                    5x
                    
                      
      exp(boot_AB_est)

                    		
                  

                  

                    223
                    
                    
                      
    })

                    		
                  

                  

                    224
                    1x
                    
                      
    res$inferential[["boot_est"]] <- tmp_boot_est

                    		
                  

                  

                    225
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    226
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    227
                    
                    
                      
  # make analysis report table

                    		
                  

                  

                    228
                    2x
                    
                      
  res$inferential[["report_overall_robustCI"]] <- rbind(

    report_table(coxobj_ipd, medSurv_ipd, tag = paste0("IPD/", endpoint_name)),

                    		
                  

                  

                    230
                    2x
                    
                      
    report_table(coxobj_ipd_adj, medSurv_ipd_adj, tag = paste0("weighted IPD/", endpoint_name)),

                    2x
                    
                      
    report_table(coxobj_agd, medSurv_agd, tag = paste0("Agd/", endpoint_name)),

    c(

                    2x
                    
                      
      paste0("** adj.", trt_ipd, " vs ", trt_agd),

      rep("-", 4),

                    		
                  

                  

                    235
                    2x
                    
                      
      print(res_AB, pval_digits = 3)

    )

                    		
                  

                  

                    237
                    
                    
                      
  )

                    2x
                    
                      
  if (is.null(res$inferential[["boot_est"]])) {

    res$inferential[["report_overall_bootCI"]] <- NULL

  } else {

                    		
                  

                  

                    242
                    1x
                    
                      
    boot_res_AB <- res_AB

                    1x
                    
                      
    boot_logres_se <- sd(log(res$inferential[["boot_est"]]), na.rm = TRUE)

    boot_res_AB$ci_l <- exp(log(boot_res_AB$est) + qnorm(0.025) * boot_logres_se)

    res$inferential[["report_overall_bootCI"]] <- rbind(

                    		
                  

                  

                    247
                    1x
                    
                      
      report_table(coxobj_ipd, medSurv_ipd, tag = paste0("IPD/", endpoint_name)),

      report_table(coxobj_ipd_adj, medSurv_ipd_adj, tag = paste0("weighted IPD/", endpoint_name)),

                    1x
                    
                      
      report_table(coxobj_agd, medSurv_agd, tag = paste0("Agd/", endpoint_name)),

                    1x
                    
                      
      c(

                    1x
                    
                      
        paste0("** adj.", trt_ipd, " vs ", trt_agd),

        rep("-", 4),

        print(boot_res_AB, pval_digits = 3)

    )

  }

                    2x
                    
                      
  res

}

                    		
                  

                
              

            

            

              

                
                  

                    1
                    
                    
                      
#' Bucher method for combining treatment effects

                    		
                  

                  

                    2
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    3
                    
                    
                      
#' Given two treatment effects of A vs. C and B vs. C

                    		
                  

                  

                    4
                    
                    
                      
#' derive the treatment effects of A vs. B using the Bucher method.

                    		
                  

                  

                    5
                    
                    
                      
#' Two-sided confidence interval and Z-test p-value are also calculated.

                    		
                  

                  

                    6
                    
                    
                      
#' Treatment effects and standard errors should be in log scale

                    		
                  

                  

                    7
                    
                    
                      
#' for hazard ratio, odds ratio, and risk ratio.

                    		
                  

                  

                    8
                    
                    
                      
#' Treatment effects and standard errors should be in natural scale

                    		
                  

                  

                    9
                    
                    
                      
#' for risk difference and mean difference.

                    		
                  

                  

                    10
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    11
                    
                    
                      
#' @param trt a list of two scalars for the study with the

                    		
                  

                  

                    12
                    
                    
                      
#' experimental arm. `'est'` is the point estimate and `'se'`

                    		
                  

                  

                    13
                    
                    
                      
#' is the standard error of the treatment effect.

                    		
                  

                  

                    14
                    
                    
                      
#' For time-to-event data, `'est'` and `'se'` should be point estimate and

                    		
                  

                  

                    15
                    
                    
                      
#' standard error of the log hazard ratio.

                    		
                  

                  

                    16
                    
                    
                      
#' For binary data, `'est'` and `'se'` should be point estimate and

                    		
                  

                  

                    17
                    
                    
                      
#' standard error of the log odds ratio, log risk ratio, or risk

                    		
                  

                  

                    18
                    
                    
                      
#' difference.

                    		
                  

                  

                    19
                    
                    
                      
#' For continuous data,  `'est'` and `'se'` should be point estimate and

                    		
                  

                  

                    20
                    
                    
                      
#' standard error of the mean difference.

                    		
                  

                  

                    21
                    
                    
                      
#' @param com same as \code{trt}, but for the study with the

                    		
                  

                  

                    22
                    
                    
                      
#' control arm

                    		
                  

                  

                    23
                    
                    
                      
#' @param conf_lv a numerical scalar, prescribe confidence level to derive

                    		
                  

                  

                    24
                    
                    
                      
#' two-sided confidence interval for the treatment effect

                    		
                  

                  

                    25
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    26
                    
                    
                      
#' @return a list with 5 elements,

                    		
                  

                  

                    27
                    
                    
                      
#' \describe{

                    		
                  

                  

                    28
                    
                    
                      
#'   \item{est}{a scalar, point estimate of the treatment effect}

                    		
                  

                  

                    29
                    
                    
                      
#'   \item{se}{a scalar, standard error of the treatment effect}

                    		
                  

                  

                    30
                    
                    
                      
#'   \item{ci_l}{a scalar, lower confidence limit of a two-sided CI

                    		
                  

                  

                    31
                    
                    
                      
#'   with prescribed nominal level by \code{conf_lv}}

                    		
                  

                  

                    32
                    
                    
                      
#'   \item{ci_u}{a scalar, upper confidence limit of a two-sided CI

                    		
                  

                  

                    33
                    
                    
                      
#'   with prescribed nominal level by \code{conf_lv}}

                    		
                  

                  

                    34
                    
                    
                      
#'   \item{pval}{p-value of Z-test, with null hypothesis that

                    		
                  

                  

                    35
                    
                    
                      
#'   \code{est} is zero}

                    		
                  

                  

                    36
                    
                    
                      
#' }

                    		
                  

                  

                    37
                    
                    
                      
#' @export

                    		
                  

                  

                    38
                    
                    
                      
#' @examples

                    		
                  

                  

                    39
                    
                    
                      
#' trt <- list(est = log(1.1), se = 0.2)

                    		
                  

                  

                    40
                    
                    
                      
#' com <- list(est = log(1.3), se = 0.18)

                    		
                  

                  

                    41
                    
                    
                      
#' result <- bucher(trt, com, conf_lv = 0.9)

                    		
                  

                  

                    42
                    
                    
                      
#' print(result, ci_digits = 3, pval_digits = 3)

                    		
                  

                  

                    43
                    
                    
                      
bucher <- function(trt, com, conf_lv = 0.95) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    44
                    4x
                    
                      
  est <- trt$est - com$est

                    		
                  

                  

                    45
                    4x
                    
                      
  se <- sqrt(trt$se^2 + com$se^2)

                    		
                  

                  

                    46
                    4x
                    
                      
  ci_l <- est - stats::qnorm(0.5 + conf_lv / 2) * se

                    		
                  

                  

                    47
                    4x
                    
                      
  ci_u <- est + stats::qnorm(0.5 + conf_lv / 2) * se

                    		
                  

                  

                    48
                    4x
                    
                      
  if (est > 0) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    49
                    !
                    
                      
    pval <- 2 * (1 - stats::pnorm(est, 0, se))

                    		
                  

                  

                    50
                    
                    
                      
  } else {

                    		
                  

                  

                    51
                    4x
                    
                      
    pval <- 2 * stats::pnorm(est, 0, se)

                    		
                  

                  

                    52
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    53
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    54
                    4x
                    
                      
  outdata <- list(

                    		
                  

                  

                    55
                    4x
                    
                      
    est = est,

                    		
                  

                  

                    56
                    4x
                    
                      
    se = se,

                    		
                  

                  

                    57
                    4x
                    
                      
    ci_l = ci_l,

                    		
                  

                  

                    58
                    4x
                    
                      
    ci_u = ci_u,

                    		
                  

                  

                    59
                    4x
                    
                      
    pval = pval

                    		
                  

                  

                    60
                    
                    
                      
  )

                    		
                  

                  

                    61
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    62
                    4x
                    
                      
  class(outdata) <- c("maicplus_bucher", "list")

                    		
                  

                  

                    63
                    4x
                    
                      
  outdata

                    		
                  

                  

                    64
                    
                    
                      
}

                    		
                  

                  

                    65
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    66
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    67
                    
                    
                      
#' Calculate standard error from the reported confidence interval.

                    		
                  

                  

                    68
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    69
                    
                    
                      
#' Comparator studies often only report confidence interval of the

                    		
                  

                  

                    70
                    
                    
                      
#' treatment effects. This function calculates standard error of the

                    		
                  

                  

                    71
                    
                    
                      
#' treatment effect given the reported confidence interval.

                    		
                  

                  

                    72
                    
                    
                      
#' For relative treatment effect (i.e. hazard ratio, odds ratio, and

                    		
                  

                  

                    73
                    
                    
                      
#' risk ratio), the function would log the confidence interval.

                    		
                  

                  

                    74
                    
                    
                      
#' For risk difference and mean difference,

                    		
                  

                  

                    75
                    
                    
                      
#' we do not log the confidence interval.

                    		
                  

                  

                    76
                    
                    
                      
#' The option to log the confidence interval is controlled

                    		
                  

                  

                    77
                    
                    
                      
#' by `'logged'` parameter.

                    		
                  

                  

                    78
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    79
                    
                    
                      
#' @param CI_lower Reported lower percentile value of the

                    		
                  

                  

                    80
                    
                    
                      
#' treatment effect

                    		
                  

                  

                    81
                    
                    
                      
#' @param CI_upper Reported upper percentile value of the

                    		
                  

                  

                    82
                    
                    
                      
#' treatment effect

                    		
                  

                  

                    83
                    
                    
                      
#' @param CI_perc Percentage of confidence interval reported

                    		
                  

                  

                    84
                    
                    
                      
#' @param logged Whether the confidence interval should be logged.

                    		
                  

                  

                    85
                    
                    
                      
#' For relative treatment effect, log should be applied because

                    		
                  

                  

                    86
                    
                    
                      
#' estimated log treatment effect is approximately normally distributed.

                    		
                  

                  

                    87
                    
                    
                      
#' @return Standard error of log relative treatment effect if `'logged'`

                    		
                  

                  

                    88
                    
                    
                      
#' is true and standard error of the treatment effect if `'logged'`

                    		
                  

                  

                    89
                    
                    
                      
#' is false

                    		
                  

                  

                    90
                    
                    
                      
#' @examples

                    		
                  

                  

                    91
                    
                    
                      
#' find_SE_from_CI(CI_lower = 0.55, CI_upper = 0.90, CI_perc = 0.95)

                    		
                  

                  

                    92
                    
                    
                      
#' @export

                    		
                  

                  

                    93
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    94
                    
                    
                      
find_SE_from_CI <- function(CI_lower = NULL, CI_upper = NULL,

                    		
                  

                  

                    95
                    
                    
                      
                            CI_perc = 0.95, logged = TRUE) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    96
                    1x
                    
                      
  if (CI_perc > 1 || CI_perc < 0) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    97
                    !
                    
                      
    stop("CI_perc has to be between 0 and 1")

                    		
                  

                  

                    98
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    99
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    100
                    1x
                    
                      
  if (is.null(CI_lower) || is.null(CI_upper)) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    101
                    !
                    
                      
    stop("Both CI_lower and CI_upper need to be specified")

                    		
                  

                  

                    102
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    103
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    104
                    1x
                    
                      
  if (!is.numeric(CI_lower) || !is.numeric(CI_upper)) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    105
                    !
                    
                      
    stop("Both CI_lower and CI_upper need to be specified")

                    		
                  

                  

                    106
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    107
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    108
                    1x
                    
                      
  alpha <- 1 - CI_perc

                    		
                  

                  

                    109
                    1x
                    
                      
  se <- ifelse(logged,

                    		
                  

                  

                    110
                    1x
                    
                      
    (log(CI_upper) - log(CI_lower)) / (2 * qnorm(1 - alpha / 2)),

                    		
                  

                  

                    111
                    1x
                    
                      
    (CI_upper - CI_lower) / (2 * qnorm(1 - alpha / 2))

                    		
                  

                  

                    112
                    
                    
                      
  )

                    		
                  

                  

                    113
                    1x
                    
                      
  return(se)

                    		
                  

                  

                    114
                    
                    
                      
}

                    		
                  

                  

                    115
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    116
                    
                    
                      
#' Print method for `maicplus_bucher` object

                    		
                  

                  

                    117
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    118
                    
                    
                      
#' @param x `maicplus_bucher` object

                    		
                  

                  

                    119
                    
                    
                      
#' @param ci_digits an integer, number of decimal places for point

                    		
                  

                  

                    120
                    
                    
                      
#' estimate and derived confidence limits

                    		
                  

                  

                    121
                    
                    
                      
#' @param pval_digits an integer, number of decimal places to display

                    		
                  

                  

                    122
                    
                    
                      
#' Z-test p-value

                    		
                  

                  

                    123
                    
                    
                      
#' @param exponentiate whether the treatment effect and confidence

                    		
                  

                  

                    124
                    
                    
                      
#' interval should be exponentiated. This applies to relative

                    		
                  

                  

                    125
                    
                    
                      
#' treatment effects. Default is set to false.

                    		
                  

                  

                    126
                    
                    
                      
#' @param ... not used

                    		
                  

                  

                    127
                    
                    
                      
#' @describeIn bucher Print method for `maicplus_bucher` objects

                    		
                  

                  

                    128
                    
                    
                      
#' @export

                    		
                  

                  

                    129
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    130
                    
                    
                      
print.maicplus_bucher <- function(x, ci_digits = 2, pval_digits = 3,

                    		
                  

                  

                    131
                    
                    
                      
                                  exponentiate = FALSE, ...) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    132
                    4x
                    
                      
  transform_this <- function(x) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    133
                    12x
                    
                      
    ifelse(exponentiate, exp(x), x)

                    		
                  

                  

                    134
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    135
                    4x
                    
                      
  a <- format(round(transform_this(x$est), ci_digits),

                    		
                  

                  

                    136
                    4x
                    
                      
    nsmall = ci_digits

                    		
                  

                  

                    137
                    
                    
                      
  )

                    		
                  

                  

                    138
                    4x
                    
                      
  b <- format(round(transform_this(x$ci_l), ci_digits),

                    		
                  

                  

                    139
                    4x
                    
                      
    nsmall = ci_digits

                    		
                  

                  

                    140
                    
                    
                      
  )

                    		
                  

                  

                    141
                    4x
                    
                      
  c <- format(round(transform_this(x$ci_u), ci_digits),

                    		
                  

                  

                    142
                    4x
                    
                      
    nsmall = ci_digits

                    		
                  

                  

                    143
                    
                    
                      
  )

                    		
                  

                  

                    144
                    4x
                    
                      
  res <- paste0(a, " [", b, "; ", c, "]")

                    		
                  

                  

                    145
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    146
                    4x
                    
                      
  disp_pval <- round(x$pval, pval_digits)

                    		
                  

                  

                    147
                    4x
                    
                      
  disp_pval <-

                    		
                  

                  

                    148
                    4x
                    
                      
    ifelse(disp_pval == 0,

                    		
                  

                  

                    149
                    4x
                    
                      
      paste0("<", 1 / (10^pval_digits)),

                    		
                  

                  

                    150
                    4x
                    
                      
      format(disp_pval, nsmall = pval_digits)

                    		
                  

                  

                    151
                    
                    
                      
    )

                    		
                  

                  

                    152
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    153
                    4x
                    
                      
  output <- c(res, disp_pval)

                    		
                  

                  

                    154
                    4x
                    
                      
  names(output) <- c("result", "pvalue")

                    		
                  

                  

                    155
                    4x
                    
                      
  print(output)

                    		
                  

                  

                    156
                    
                    
                      
}

                    		
                  

                
              

            

            

              

                
                  

                    1
                    
                    
                      
#' Generate time-to-event data

                    		
                  

                  

                    2
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    3
                    
                    
                      
#' Function generates time-to-event data. We follow the data-generating mechanism from

                    		
                  

                  

                    4
                    
                    
                      
#' Bender et al. and Remiro-Azocar et al. 2021 to simulate Weibull-distributed survival times

                    		
                  

                  

                    5
                    
                    
                      
#' under a proportional hazards parameterization. As per Remiro-Azocar et al, we set the

                    		
                  

                  

                    6
                    
                    
                      
#' default scale parameter (lambda) to 8.5 and shape parameter (nu) to 1.3 to reflect frequently

                    		
                  

                  

                    7
                    
                    
                      
#' observed mortality trends in metastatic cancer patients. Censoring times are generated from

                    		
                  

                  

                    8
                    
                    
                      
#' exponential distribution where the rate parameter is 0.96 is selected to achieve a censoring rate

                    		
                  

                  

                    9
                    
                    
                      
#' of 35% under the active treatment at baseline (with the values of the covariates set to zero).

                    		
                  

                  

                    10
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    11
                    
                    
                      
#' @param N sample size

                    		
                  

                  

                    12
                    
                    
                      
#' @param ncov number of covariates to generate

                    		
                  

                  

                    13
                    
                    
                      
#' @param lambda scale parameter in baseline hazard function

                    		
                  

                  

                    14
                    
                    
                      
#' @param nu shape parameter in baseline hazard function

                    		
                  

                  

                    15
                    
                    
                      
#' @param censor_rate rate parameter of the exponential distribution of censoring times

                    		
                  

                  

                    16
                    
                    
                      
#' @param cor correlation between covariates

                    		
                  

                  

                    17
                    
                    
                      
#' @param marginal_mean marginal mean of covariates

                    		
                  

                  

                    18
                    
                    
                      
#' @param marginal_sd marginal standard deviation of covariates

                    		
                  

                  

                    19
                    
                    
                      
#' @param beta vector of coefficients for prognostic factors. Defaults is `-log(0.67)` for all covariates.

                    		
                  

                  

                    20
                    
                    
                      
#' @param gamma vector of coefficients for effect modifiers. Default is `0` for half of the covariates and

                    		
                  

                  

                    21
                    
                    
                      
#'  `-log(0.67)` for the others.

                    		
                  

                  

                    22
                    
                    
                      
#' @param d0 coefficient for the treatment effect for patients with `treat = 0`

                    		
                  

                  

                    23
                    
                    
                      
#' @param seed seed used for simulation reproducibility

                    		
                  

                  

                    24
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    25
                    
                    
                      
#' @return data.frame with survival time, censor (event) status, treatment indicator, and covariates

                    		
                  

                  

                    26
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    27
                    
                    
                      
#' @references Remiro-Azocar et al. 2021

                    		
                  

                  

                    28
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    29
                    
                    
                      
#' @export

                    		
                  

                  

                    30
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    31
                    
                    
                      
generate_survival_data <- function(N = 150, ncov = 4, lambda = 8.5, nu = 1.3, censor_rate = 0.96,

                    		
                  

                  

                    32
                    
                    
                      
                                   cor = 0.35, marginal_mean = 0.6, marginal_sd = 0.2,

                    		
                  

                  

                    33
                    
                    
                      
                                   beta = rep(-log(0.67), ncov),

                    		
                  

                  

                    34
                    
                    
                      
                                   gamma = sort(rep(c(0, -log(0.67)), length = ncov)),

                    		
                  

                  

                    35
                    
                    
                      
                                   d0 = log(0.25), seed = 1) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    36
                    !
                    
                      
  set.seed(seed)

                    		
                  

                  

                    37
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    38
                    
                    
                      
  # if beta and gamma is not specified, give it default values

                    		
                  

                  

                    39
                    !
                    
                      
  if (is.null(beta)) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    40
                    !
                    
                      
    beta <- rep(-log(0.67), ncov)

                    		
                  

                  

                    41
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    42
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    43
                    !
                    
                      
  if (is.null(gamma)) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    44
                    !
                    
                      
    gamma <- rep(-log(0.67), ncov)

                    		
                  

                  

                    45
                    !
                    
                      
    gamma[1:round(ncov / 2)] <- 0

                    		
                  

                  

                    46
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    47
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    48
                    
                    
                      
  # generate ncov covariates (X) using a multivariate normal

                    		
                  

                  

                    49
                    !
                    
                      
  sigma <- matrix(cor, nrow = ncov, ncol = ncov)

                    		
                  

                  

                    50
                    !
                    
                      
  diag(sigma) <- 1

                    		
                  

                  

                    51
                    !
                    
                      
  sigma <- sigma * marginal_sd^2

                    		
                  

                  

                    52
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    53
                    !
                    
                      
  covariates <- MASS::mvrnorm(N, mu = rep(marginal_mean, ncov), Sigma = sigma)

                    		
                  

                  

                    54
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    55
                    !
                    
                      
  treat <- sample(x = c(0, 1), size = N, replace = TRUE, prob = c(0.5, 0.5))

                    		
                  

                  

                    56
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    57
                    
                    
                      
  # linear predictor

                    		
                  

                  

                    58
                    !
                    
                      
  lp <- covariates %*% beta + covariates %*% gamma * treat + d0 * treat

                    		
                  

                  

                    59
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    60
                    
                    
                      
  # Weibull latent event times

                    		
                  

                  

                    61
                    !
                    
                      
  u <- runif(n = N)

                    		
                  

                  

                    62
                    !
                    
                      
  latent_time <- (-log(u) / (lambda * exp(lp)))^(1 / nu)

                    		
                  

                  

                    63
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    64
                    
                    
                      
  # exponential censoring times

                    		
                  

                  

                    65
                    !
                    
                      
  censor_time <- rexp(n = N, rate = censor_rate)

                    		
                  

                  

                    66
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    67
                    
                    
                      
  # follow-up times and event indicators

                    		
                  

                  

                    68
                    !
                    
                      
  time <- pmin(latent_time, censor_time)

                    		
                  

                  

                    69
                    !
                    
                      
  event <- as.numeric(latent_time <= censor_time)

                    		
                  

                  

                    70
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    71
                    !
                    
                      
  colnames(covariates) <- paste0("x", seq_len(ncov))

                    		
                  

                  

                    72
                    !
                    
                      
  survival_data <- data.frame(USUBJID = seq_len(N), time = time, event = event, treat = treat, x = covariates)

                    		
                  

                  

                    73
                    !
                    
                      
  return(survival_data)

                    		
                  

                  

                    74
                    
                    
                      
}

#' helper function: sort out a nice report table to summarize survival analysis results

                    		
                  

                  

                    2
                    
                    
                      
#' for `maic_tte_unanchor`

                    		
                  

                  

                    3
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    4
                    
                    
                      
#' @param coxobj returned object from \code{\link[survival]{coxph}}

                    		
                  

                  

                    5
                    
                    
                      
#' @param medSurvobj returned object from \code{\link{medSurv_makeup}}

                    		
                  

                  

                    6
                    
                    
                      
#' @param tag a string, by default NULL, if specified, an extra 1st column is created in the output

                    		
                  

                  

                    7
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    8
                    
                    
                      
#' @return a data frame with sample size, incidence rate, median survival time with 95% CI, hazard ratio estimate with

                    		
                  

                  

                    9
                    
                    
                      
#' 95% CI and Wald test of hazard ratio

                    		
                  

                  

                    10
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    11
                    
                    
                      
#' @export

                    		
                  

                  

                    12
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    13
                    
                    
                      
report_table <- function(coxobj, medSurvobj, tag = NULL) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    14
                    9x
                    
                      
  hr_res <- format(round(summary(coxobj)$conf.int[-2], 2), nsmall = 2)

                    		
                  

                  

                    15
                    9x
                    
                      
  hr_res <- paste0(hr_res[1], "[", hr_res[2], ";", hr_res[3], "]")

                    		
                  

                  

                    16
                    9x
                    
                      
  hr_pval <- format(round(summary(coxobj)$waldtest[3], 3), nsmall = 3)

                    		
                  

                  

                    17
                    9x
                    
                      
  if (hr_pval == "0.000") hr_pval <- "<0.001"

                    		
                  

                  

                    18
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    19
                    9x
                    
                      
  meds_report <- format(round(medSurvobj[, c("median", "0.95LCL", "0.95UCL")], 1), nsmall = 1)

                    		
                  

                  

                    20
                    9x
                    
                      
  meds_report <- apply(meds_report, 1, function(xx) paste0(xx[1], "[", xx[2], ";", xx[3], "]"))

                    		
                  

                  

                    21
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    22
                    9x
                    
                      
  desc_res <- cbind(medSurvobj[, "treatment", drop = FALSE],

                    		
                  

                  

                    23
                    9x
                    
                      
    data.frame(N = round(medSurvobj$n.max, 1)),

                    		
                  

                  

                    24
                    9x
                    
                      
    "n.events(%)" = paste0(

                    		
                  

                  

                    25
                    9x
                    
                      
      round(medSurvobj$events, 1), "(",

                    		
                  

                  

                    26
                    9x
                    
                      
      format(round(medSurvobj$events * 100 / medSurvobj$n.max, 1), nsmall = 1), ")"

                    		
                  

                  

                    27
                    
                    
                      
    ),

                    		
                  

                  

                    28
                    9x
                    
                      
    "median[95% CI]" = meds_report

                    		
                  

                  

                    29
                    
                    
                      
  )

                    		
                  

                  

                    30
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    31
                    9x
                    
                      
  desc_res <- cbind(desc_res[c(2, 1), ], "HR[95% CI]" = c(hr_res, ""), "p-Value" = c(hr_pval, ""))

                    		
                  

                  

                    32
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    33
                    9x
                    
                      
  if (!is.null(tag)) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    34
                    9x
                    
                      
    desc_res <- cbind(data.frame(Matching = rep(tag, nrow(desc_res))), desc_res)

                    		
                  

                  

                    35
                    9x
                    
                      
    desc_res$Matching[duplicated(desc_res$Matching)] <- ""

                    		
                  

                  

                    36
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    37
                    9x
                    
                      
  desc_res

                    		
                  

                  

                    38
                    
                    
                      
}

#' Get and Set Time Conversion Factors

                    		
                  

                  

                    5
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    6
                    
                    
                      
#' @param days Factor to divide data time units to get time in days

                    		
                  

                  

                    7
                    
                    
                      
#' @param weeks Factor to divide data time units to get time in weeks

                    		
                  

                  

                    8
                    
                    
                      
#' @param months Factor to divide data time units to get time in months

                    		
                  

                  

                    9
                    
                    
                      
#' @param years Factor to divide data time units to get time in years

                    		
                  

                  

                    10
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    11
                    
                    
                      
#' @return No value returned. Conversion factors are stored internally and used within functions.

                    		
                  

                  

                    12

                    13
                    
                    
                      
#' @rdname time_conversion

                    		
                  

                  

                    14

                    15

                    16
                    
                    
                      
#' # Native time format is years

                    		
                  

                  

                    17
                    
                    
                      
#' set_time_conversion(days = 1 / 365.25, weeks = 1 / 52.17857, months = 1 / 12, years = 1)

                    		
                  

                  

                    18
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    19
                    
                    
                      
#' # Native time format is days

                    		
                  

                  

                    20
                    
                    
                      
#' set_time_conversion(days = 1, weeks = 7, months = 365.25 / 12, years = 365.25)

                    		
                  

                  

                    21
                    
                    
                      
set_time_conversion <- function(days = 1, weeks = 7, months = 365.25 / 12, years = 365.25) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    22
                    !
                    
                      
  settings_env$time_conversion <- c(days = days, weeks = weeks, months = months, years = years)

                    		
                  

                  

                    23
                    
                    
                      
}

                    		
                  

                  

                    24
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    25
                    
                    
                      

                    		
                  

                  

                    26
                    
                    
                      
#' @param factor Time factor to get.

                    		
                  

                  

                    27
                    
                    
                      
#' @rdname time_conversion

                    		
                  

                  

                    28
                    
                    
                      
#' @export

                    		
                  

                  

                    29
                    
                    
                      
#'

                    		
                  

                  

                    30
                    
                    
                      
#' @examples

                    		
                  

                  

                    31
                    
                    
                      
#' # Get time scale factors:

                    		
                  

                  

                    32
                    
                    
                      
#' get_time_conversion("years")

                    		
                  

                  

                    33
                    
                    
                      
#' get_time_conversion("weeks")

                    		
                  

                  

                    34
                    
                    
                      
get_time_conversion <- function(factor = c("days", "weeks", "months", "years")) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    35
                    6x
                    
                      
  factor <- match.arg(factor, several.ok = TRUE)

                    		
                  

                  

                    36
                    6x
                    
                      
  if (!exists("time_conversion", settings_env)) {

                    		
                  

                  

                    37
                    !
                    
                      
    warning("No time conversion factors previously set. Setting defaults.")

                    		
                  

                  

                    38
                    !
                    
                      
    set_time_conversion()

                    		
                  

                  

                    39
                    
                    
                      
  }

                    		
                  

                  

                    40
                    6x
                    
                      
  settings_env$time_conversion[factor]

                    		
                  

                  

                    41
                    
                    
                      
}
